function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

if (is_file('3p/vts_fileformats/LICENSE') && (sha1_file('3p/vts_fileformats/LICENSE') != '71fa3747ca3c8855ee9813fbd6cadb934181a901')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/vts_fileformats/LICENSE');
	$tmp = pathinfo('3p/vts_fileformats/LICENSE');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/vts_fileformats/LICENSE')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('3p/vts_fileformats/LICENSE', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('3p/vts_fileformats/LICENSE')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/vts_fileformats/LICENSE');
} else if (sha1_file('3p/vts_fileformats/LICENSE') != '71fa3747ca3c8855ee9813fbd6cadb934181a901') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/vts_fileformats/LICENSE');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/vts_fileformats/LICENSE', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/vts_fileformats/LICENSE');
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: 3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js') != '9a88f13a13b979964a91fede3b679818aa33c212') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js') !== '9a88f13a13b979964a91fede3b679818aa33c212') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js') !== '36bbc98b10e364c10b61c4460b26b873dec2734a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js') !== '9a88f13a13b979964a91fede3b679818aa33c212') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/layout/jquery.layout_and_plugins.js');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php') != '26e238544a8d2a485e7f026872dd81d4455249be') {

	}

}

@unlink('3p/minify/Dockerfile');
if (is_file('3p/minify/Dockerfile')) {
	warn('File could not be deleted: 3p/minify/Dockerfile');
}

// File deleted: 3p/minify/docker-compose.yml
@unlink('3p/minify/docker-compose.yml');
if (is_file('3p/minify/docker-compose.yml')) {
	warn('File could not be deleted: 3p/minify/docker-compose.yml');
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 528\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 528') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
